 function onSearchText()
 {
 const searchIconButton = document.getElementById("header-search-button");
 const dropdown = document.getElementById("header-select");
 const searchInput = document.getElementById("search-text");
 if (searchIconButton && dropdown && searchInput) {
 searchIconButton.addEventListener("click", function () {
 const dropdownValue = dropdown.value;
 const keyword = encodeURIComponent(searchInput.value.trim());
 let url = "";
 if (dropdownValue === "Blogs") {
 url = `https://sigmaearth.com/?s=${keyword}`;
 } else if (dropdownValue === "Jobs") {
 url = `https://sigmaearth.com/sustainability-jobs/jobs/?search_keywords=${keyword}&search_region=0&search_category=0`;
 }
 else if (dropdownValue === "Courses") {
 url = `https://sigmaearth.com/environmental-courses/courses/?c_search=${keyword}&ref=course`;
 }
 else if (dropdownValue === "Eco-Listing") {
 url = `https://sigmaearth.com/eco-friendly-sustainable-products-services/ads/?keyword=${keyword}`;
 }
 else{
 url = `https://sigmaearth.com/?s=${keyword}`;
 }
 if (url) {
 window.open(url, "_blank"); // open in new tab
 }
 });
 }
}

 {
 const searchIconButton = document.getElementById("search-category-button");
 const searchInput = document.getElementById("search-category-id");
 if (searchIconButton && searchInput) {
 const keyword = encodeURIComponent(searchInput.value.trim());
 url = `https://sigmaearth.com/?s=${keyword}&et_pb_searchform_submit=et_search_proccess&et_pb_include_posts=yes`; 
 if (url) {
 window.open(url, "_blank"); // open in new tab
 }
 }
}
 function getCollection()
 {
 const searchIconButton = document.getElementById("collection-select");
 if (searchIconButton) {
 const keyword = searchIconButton.value;
 var url="";
 switch(keyword)
 {
 case "Trending":url="https://sigmaearth.com/category/trending/";
 break;
 case "Climate Crisis":url="https://sigmaearth.com/category/environmental-news/climate-crisis/";
 break;
 case "Electric Vehicles":url="https://sigmaearth.com/category/green-investments/electric-vehicles/";
 break;
 case "Solar Energy":url="https://sigmaearth.com/category/renewable-energy/solar-energy/";
 break;
 case "Sustainable Fashion":url="https://sigmaearth.com/category/sustainability/sustainable-fashion/";
 break;
 case "Glossary and FAQs":url="https://sigmaearth.com/category/glossary-and-faq/";
 break;
 default:url="https://sigmaearth.com/environmental-topics-new/";
 break; 
 } 
 if (url) {
 window.open(url, "_blank"); // open in new tab
 }
 }
}

 return;

 }
 }

 delete dropdown.dataset.lastkey;
